They helped you, they were here at a certain time and added something to your life. They were not meant to stay for longer than that but celebrate the short moment and let them go. They were on your road to help you at one moment of your life. You will find other friends who will follow you and walk at your side forever. <p>•I talk more quietly than normal</p>

<p>•I don’t talk abt myself at all</p>

<p>•I make cynical comments, especially abt my existence</p>

<p>•I sleep too much or too little</p>



<p>this is not just me, though. these are common signs/things to be aware of and look for in people/friends/family members struggling w depression. stay safe, and stay aware.</p></blockquote>
<p><a href="http://papi-flacko.tumblr.com/post/139371724417/some-people-spend-their-life-searching-for-love" class="tumblr_blog">papi-flacko</a>:</p>

<blockquote><p>some people spend their life searching for love</p>

<p>some people spend their life running away from love</p>

<p>some people don’t know what love is</p></blockquote>
<p><a href="http://this-little-reject.tumblr.com/post/139387773657/i-feel-honored-and-privileged-to-say-that" class="tumblr_blog">this-little-reject</a>:</p>

<blockquote><p>I feel honored and privileged to say that <a class="tumblelog" href="http://tmblr.co/mcAk5-6rheOOS-FCXUkPJ9Q">@skinny-love-just-last-the-year-x</a>   is my best friend. She is the most kindest,accepting, caring, generous and gorgeous person I have ever known. She has helped me through so much and always knows how to make me smile. She is the kind of human being that everyone needs in their life. I’m so happy that I decided to message you that day on tumblr because if I didn’t I wouldn’t be able to call you my best friend. I love you Rachel and I hope to see you this summer.💖</p>

<p>-Love Hanna (this-little-reject)</p></blockquote>

<p>OMG I LOVE YOU 💜</p>
<p><a href="http://this-little-reject.tumblr.com/post/131042165277/skinny-love-just-last-the-year-x-i-can-smell-your" class="tumblr_blog">this-little-reject</a>:</p>

<blockquote><p><a class="tumblelog" href="http://tmblr.co/mcAk5-6rheOOS-FCXUkPJ9Q">@skinny-love-just-last-the-year-x</a> I can smell your filthy soul</p></blockquote>

<p>TRU</p>
<p><a href="http://this-little-reject.tumblr.com/post/131042012832/skinny-love-just-last-the-year-x-is-making-so" class="tumblr_blog">this-little-reject</a>:</p>

<blockquote><p><a class="tumblelog" href="http://tmblr.co/mcAk5-6rheOOS-FCXUkPJ9Q">@skinny-love-just-last-the-year-x</a> is making so many <a class="tumblelog" href="http://tmblr.co/mCCuOqEAeE46UWAHsnkmBXQ">@5sos-official</a> jokes oh my shit</p></blockquote>
